<Response>None< /Response><review>This is the real deal folks. It's so hard getting good Mexican here in Humboldt and I'm glad to say I have finally found it. First there is a salsa bar. That alone should be enough to come and visit. But let me tell you this place has the best tortilla chips around. Thick and crunchy and warm. A+++

The food is also top notch. With good portions at a price where you won't feel like your getting ripped off for a couple tacos with beans and rice. Speaking of beans and rice this place delivers. Thick and rich refried beans and rice strait out of southern California (old Mexicao üòâ).

There are also plenty of filling choices for those tacos and burritos including all the normal Mexican meats and also a verity of vegan and vegetarian options...great job!

It's a tiny but out of town (Humboldt hill) but the restaurant is cute with lots of light and plant life. If you haven't been here yet and are a fan of Mexican food give it a try. You won't be disappointed.< /review><Rating>5<//Rating><Time>1552189407022< /Time>< user_id>

<rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Came in for a shave and hair cut. Hair cut turned out good but the shave was not what I hoped for and was left with stubble. I was under the impression that a hot towel would be used before applying the shaving cream, it wasn't, in fact no hot towel was used at all.

From the outside, this place does not look like much.Inside, theres modern look to with old style wood cabinets, flat screen television, surround sound and stain glass which adds a nice touch to the place. It's also clean with comfortable seating.

Haircut $11= Good Deal
Shave $11 = This would also be a good deal if hot towels were used. Therefore, it should be $5.

They seem to be expanding the shop. This could result price increase at some point in time.</Review>

A great place to get seafood. A warning to those that do go for the first time  go super hungry or bring a friend to share.

My fav is either the surf and.turf: a burrito with carne asada and shrimp with rice.l and guac The shrimp are not your small nail sized shrimp, so it's worth going for.

The other thing I get is the Delmar fish and shrimp burrito made  with rice, lettuce dressed with tartar sauce and salsa.

I have been going for years and since leaving San Diego 20 yrs ago I still go back.<//text>

<text>I am the first to admit that I am not a "go with the flow" bride and that I need to have every detail understood and taken care of to be satisfied. In the last year of planning my wedding, Galway Downs has bent over backwards and forwards in helping me get through this process despite Covid. Yes you need to make some sacrifice if you insist on getting married during this time, for example, the buffet is not going to be self-serve, a partition will be there and someone will serve the guests as they walk down the buffet line. These are the rules of the government, not the venue. They do not cancel your wedding date because of Covid and not refund you. You have the option of rescheduling your wedding on a different day using the same deposit for up to one year. If you have booked and need to cancel for whatever reason, the reality is that the contract literally addresses "pandemics" in their policy. This is business. Expecting not to be charged for a certain amount  (that you have agreed on) while having your wedding take up a Saturday for the last X months, then to decide to reschedule based on Covid regulations you feel don't fit with the vision of your wedding and then be upset because you didn't get your down payment refunded is indicative you have very limited knowledge on how businesses must operate. You have taken up a Saturday wedding slot away form all the hundreds of other brides freaking out about finding a venue for their wedding. This has not been my experience but I feel strongly enough about how great everyone at Wedgwood is and how they're doing everything in their power to help me have my dream wedding. They respond to my micro-managed repetitive emails so quickly! They answer all my questions and send me photos because I need to know what their tea cups look like, I need to know how many people will be picking up dirty plates, and I need to know if I can get to the venue as early as I am asking in order to calm my nerves the day of the wedding. Galway Downs has given me ALL of the things I'm asking for. They want you to have a wonderful wedding!!! <Time>1616002792012<//Time><rating>5<//rating><review>different optometrists as I changed my jobs at locations, although still in the bay area but at distances from Fremont.  I have always been very careful on choosing the best possible optometrist as my prescriptions are fairly deep and I am very carefully on taking care of my eyes. I am in micro-optics industry, working on tiny optics and components. I examine my eyes every year and change my glasses every two years.
In recent years I have gradually found that the new glasses cannot bring my vision back. I had brought this issue to my optometrist who then had tried different prescriptions to resolve the issue. My prescriptions are getting deeper and deeper, with astigmatisms adding on. But I still suffer the same problem.
When I came back to Dr. Pirrone in 2018 for a consultation, she immediately fund out the problem with my eyes after a thorough examination and introduced me to an eye surgent. During the period of choosing the right amount of correction at surgery, I had consulted Dr. Pirrone several times and she had given me many suggestions and performed many tests to settled down the right corrections for the surgery, and calmed down my anxiety.
Now I am vision is completely back and I am very happy with the surgery result. Dr. Pirrone is far more than a top-notch optometrist. She loves her job and she really cares about her patents!< /review>< pics>

<Name>Michael Uribe</Name><Pictures>None</Pictures><Review>Okay so this was my first time to a bingo parlor so take my review with a grain of salt.  On the outside the place is pretty nice, plenty of parking and well lit.  The inside is nothing special, just a giant room with long rows of tables setup.  There is a small food bar to get food and drinks, an outside patio to smoke and play at the same time, and an announcers booth.  There are also people that go around with food and drink carts in case you don't want to leave your seat.

Now I don't know about other bingo places but this place was fast paced!  Like super fast paced.  The show the number on the screen and announce it and immediately move along.  There were some times I wasn't able to keep up and missed some numbers because of it.  They play several games, each winning you $250 with some special games of $500.  The crowd is mainly older but very friendly.  I didn't win anything but still had a pretty good time.  I wouldn't recommend this place for beginners like myself, it's just too fast paced and confusing when you are still trying to learn the game.  If you're a seasoned bingo pro then this is the place for you.< /Review>< userid>

<userid>101017571565168915935<//userid><user_name>Jennifer Gallego<//user_name><date>1469902376800< /date><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
If you can handle how fast they go than you'll love it. Games are $1-$2 depending with payouts between $250-500 depending on the day and time that you go. The Pull Tabs pay between $250-$1500, but most pay $1199.  More often than not your fellow players sitting around you will help you if your not sure how to play anday even spot a Bingo before you do. The food is what you would find at a food truck and is ok if your really hungry but they have free coffee, tea, and water of course. There's also a smoking section if that's what you're in to. We go often and we've won often. What can I say? It's addicting.<//Review>
